         -moz-column-count: 2;
              column-count: 2; } }

      -webkit-column-count: 3;
         -moz-column-count: 3;
              column-count: 3; } }

      -webkit-column-count: 4;
         -moz-column-count: 4;
              column-count: 4; } }

    margin: 0 0 1em 0;

       page-break-inside: avoid;
            break-inside: avoid; }

    padding: 0; }

    color: #000000; }
  main a[href^=http]:after {
    content: " (" attr(href) ") "; }
  main a[href^="#"]:after, main a.uzk15__imagelink:after {
    content: ""; }

    float: none;
    clear: both;
